dropping almost 2 miles out of the sky to raise money for Project Stand By Me...&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Project Stand By Me is an innovative and creative system of services for children and adults with neurological conditions and a support network for their family members and carers. &lt;br /&gt; The idea of the project was created by Judit Szathmry and Amanda Elliott who both trained and worked in the field of Conductive Education (The Pet&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt; System of rehabilitation).&lt;br /&gt; Incorporating Conductive Education Project Stand By Me will offer a number of beneficial and inspiring services for children, adults and their families. &lt;br /&gt; To achieve this Project Stand By Me is currently in the process of securing funds for a building where the project will be based. All money raised from Mandy&#039;s skydive will go towards this. &lt;br /&gt; A 25 sponsor will buy a brick for the building. All sponsors names will be engraved on a special plaque on the building. &lt;br /&gt; Thank you for your support and please help us spread the word! &lt;i class="_4-k1 img sp_fM-mz8spZ1b recently become a trustee for a new Project Project Stand By Me. To be able to make this fantastic idea a reality we need to raise funds to support the different services available. If you are able to help us out with this by donating no matter how big or small this would be hugely appreciated. This is something incredibly close to my heart as I been attending conductive education sessions in the New Forest with the amazing Judit and Mandy since I was around 7 years old and the effect it has had on my life has been incredible, without it I honestly believe I wouldn&#039;t have half of what I do today and I believe that others should be able to have access to these fantastic services and opportunities. data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div id="id_55a52d71e78cc6347622957" class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;p&gt;Member of Advisory Panel: Susie Mallett&lt;br /&gt; &#039;I am an artist, art therapist, conductor, writer and publisher. I am English and I live and do most of my work in Germany.&lt;br /&gt; Conductive pedagogy and upbringing have been my passion since I first discovered them in 1986.&lt;br /&gt; In my role as a conductor I have always believed that it is my responsibility when working with my clients, their carers, families, teachers etc., to help them to develop all aspects of their lives in the ways that they w&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt;ish. My role is to encourage clients to discover what it is that motivates them to lead active lives and then together we can find ways to achieve this activity and by doing so create happy, healthy souls.&lt;br /&gt; Whether this is achieved through writing, reading, walking in the countryside, cooking, sewing, papier-mch, painting, drawing, photography, music or something completely different, what matters is that the clients and other people sharing their lives strive towards a fulfilled and happy life.&lt;br /&gt; I am very glad that through Projectstandbyme a wider network can be built up linking people involved with conductive lifestyles to achieve goals that inspire them.&lt;br /&gt; As Judit says  Everyone needs someone to stand by them. &lt;br /&gt; By connecting people in this way, people with many different needs, aspirations and creative skills, there are no limits to what could be achieved.&#039;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt; &lt;span data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div id="id_55a52d71e85c04462634476" class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;p&gt;Member of Advisory Panel: Vishali Malhotra&lt;br /&gt; My name is Vishali Malhotra and I am a conductor and director of Beyond NeuroDevelopment Inc. (Toronto, Canada). Each day brings a smile to my face, as I have the pleasure of working with such amazing individuals and their support teams, helping everyone reach his or her personal best. When people say the work of a conductor is very rewarding, I agree with them, as I have learnt just as much from the individuals Ive worked with over&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt; the years, as they have from me.I am proud to be a part of the Project Stand By Me Advisory Panel, as I believe together we can help individuals and their families prepare for key transitional stages in life. I love the idea of connecting with so many people to make this possible, so we can ultimately make a positive ripple effect around the world. Change can be exciting, often necessary, and very possible!&lt;br /&gt; Vishali Malhotra, B.A. (Hons) Conductive Education, QCS&lt;br /&gt; Conductor and Director of Beyond Neurodevelopment Inc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class="text_exposed_show"&gt;&lt;p&gt; Genius &lt;a href="http://l.facebook.com/l.php?u=http%3A%2F%2FQuotes.net%2F&amp;h=7AQHYIaXK&amp;enc=AZNF9gZOu8w6u4mamAYDZn1VhQzmoNQ-DHNJZdy6AOZFvS2cPd6F2SUZp2i5jQk8Jd4-YqBrb4-p71nOTrSxxks4wx6VraF4q9w-pgdSGuY10x7fDwD3NQiYAmxjw2LxZlLN4a9p8xWaU38ye3MDSin17prrkRiP0O-B9ULurXbWEckj0c2SLZ6C0GPkF3fBqLE4ucGp9wiUXS5zbk2u8GKy&amp;s=1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow" onmouseover="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\\/\\/Quotes.net\\/&quot;);" onclick="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\\/\\/l.facebook.com\\/l.php?u=http\\u00253A\\u00252F\\u00252FQuotes.net\\u00252F&amp;h=7AQHYIaXK&amp;enc=AZNF9gZOu8w6u4mamAYDZn1VhQzmoNQ-DHNJZdy6AOZFvS2cPd6F2SUZp2i5jQk8Jd4-YqBrb4-p71nOTrSxxks4wx6VraF4q9w-pgdSGuY10x7fDwD3NQiYAmxjw2LxZlLN4a9p8xWaU38ye3MDSin17prrkRiP0O-B9ULurXbWEckj0c2SLZ6C0GPkF3fBqLE4ucGp9wiUXS5zbk2u8GKy&amp;s=1&quot;);"&gt;Quotes.net&lt;/a&gt; (2014, May 27) Genius Quotes- Unique Quotes and Saying. added &lt;a href="/permalink.php?story_fbid=773236182762136&amp;id=749904855095269"&gt;3 new photos&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;&lt;div class="_5pcp"&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span class="fsm fwn fcg"&gt;&lt;a class="_5pcq" href="/permalink.php?story_fbid=773236182762136&amp;id=749904855095269" target=""&gt;&lt;abbr title="Wednesday, February 11, 2015 at 7:03am" data-utime="1423667018" data-shorten="1" class="_5ptz"&gt;February 11&lt;/abbr&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  &lt;span&gt;&lt;a data-hover="tooltip" aria-label="Show edit history" class="uiLinkSubtle" ajaxify="/ajax/edits/browser/post/?content_token=773236182762136" rel="dialog" href="#" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;+E&quot;&#125;" role="button"&gt;Edited&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;  &lt;a data-hover="tooltip" aria-label="Public" class="uiStreamPrivacy inlineBlock fbStreamPrivacy fbPrivacyAudienceIndicator _5pcq" href="#" role="button"&gt;&lt;i class="lock img sp_VTao_RYfyVB sx_44fe27"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"&gt;&lt;div id="id_55a52d71e88640348876268" class="text_exposed_root"&gt;&lt;p&gt;Challenge Me! TM Mobility Activity Cards designed by Amanda Elliott                                                                                                Amanda Elliott the creator of the Challange Me!TM Mobility and Activity Cards is a senior conductor, one of the first graduates of the National Institute of Conductive Education UK.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; The set of beautifully illustrated full-colour mobility cards, together with a detailed instruction booklet, is a valuable tool for all&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt; professionals and parents facilitating the rehabilitation of children with neurological disorders and general developmental disabilities.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class="text_exposed_show"&gt;&lt;p&gt; The activities address the development of mobility and coordination skills, while also promoting independence and self-esteem, using a fun approach that is motivating for children.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; The cards were designed to give parents and professionals plenty of new ideas of tasks to practise at home/school to help improve mobility and all over motor skills based on Conductive Education.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Using the cards is fun and provide you with many useful ideas how to help children to improve essential skills. The cards also enable children to choose, focus, plan, empowering them to take charge in their own problem solving in a playful way.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Children can create their own activity regime which they can practice every day until they master the skills required, or they can choose ad-hoc challenges throughout the day which will build their abilities.&lt;br /&gt; The cards were created in mind that everyone involved with child care, upbringing and education can easily be involved in helping children in a relaxed and joyful way.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; In her resource review Julie Hughes of Down Syndrome Education International writes about the Challenge Me! Mobility Activity Cards.&lt;br /&gt; &quot;I&#039;m always on the look-out for useful, practical activities that can be worked into everyday games  and that is just what I found in these cards.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; The Challenge Me! Mobility Activity Cards - a set of useful, practical activities that can be worked into everyday games. They address mobility, balance coordination, spatial awareness, trunk control, transferring skills, gross motor skills, flexibility, adaptability, safety awareness, and independence. Practising these skills can also have a knock-on effect on self-esteem and confidence.&quot;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; Link to full article: &lt;a href="http://l.facebook.com/l.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.down-syndrome.org%2Fresources%2F2023%2F&amp;h=iAQG_wjEY&amp;enc=AZPZW6PmWsVWs91WZd-77dmAskear9WHDxEI9Sn2e6wB7QQUrdDsrUSRKaW4smIy8iEmC55jAq8unOPKmdJ5Pou1fgGdiL0cieseda6A3p1BIOMRiKZOHEAK1E6sdrYvQjMxCmJdXxWkbNg2xI2SxpN9enJ1apAequrA9jr8s14KPn_hebZ3FO4Pahduhp0SFl-Ie1KGIrs_XwP4FSMWKxPs&amp;s=1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow" onmouseover="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\\/\\/www.down-syndrome.org\\/resources\\/2023\\/&quot;);" onclick="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\\/\\/l.facebook.com\\/l.php?u=http\\u00253A\\u00252F\\u00252Fwww.down-syndrome.org\\u00252Fresources\\u00252F2023\\u00252F&amp;h=iAQG_wjEY&amp;enc=AZPZW6PmWsVWs91WZd-77dmAskear9WHDxEI9Sn2e6wB7QQUrdDsrUSRKaW4smIy8iEmC55jAq8unOPKmdJ5Pou1fgGdiL0cieseda6A3p1BIOMRiKZOHEAK1E6sdrYvQjMxCmJdXxWkbNg2xI2SxpN9enJ1apAequrA9jr8s14KPn_hebZ3FO4Pahduhp0SFl-Ie1KGIrs_XwP4FSMWKxPs&amp;s=1&quot;);"&gt;http://www.down-syndrome.org/resources/2023/&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;
